ModelDNN_FlexibleLayers(
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)
ModelDNN_3layers(
  (fc1): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=2048, bias=True)
  (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
  (fc3): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)

  (ln2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)
ModelVGG(
  (cnn_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (3): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (4): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (5): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (6): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (7): ReLU(inplace=True)
  )
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=5248, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((5248,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=5248, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)
ModelDNN_5layers(

  (fc4): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=128, bias=True)

ModelAlexNet(
  (cnn_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)

    (2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (3): ReLU(inplace=True)

    (5): ReLU(inplace=True)
  )
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(

    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

ModelCNN_LSTM(
  (conv1): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (conv2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (convs): Sequential(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): ReLU()
    (3): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (5): ReLU()
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, batch_first=True)
  (fc1): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=2048, bias=True)
  (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
  (fc3): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  (ln1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (ln2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

  (conv1): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (conv2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (convs): Sequential(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): ReLU()
    (3): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (5): ReLU()
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, batch_first=True)
  (fc1): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=2048, bias=True)
  (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
  (fc3): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)

  (ln2): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

ModelLeNet(
  (cnn_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (3): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (5): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (6): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (7): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (8): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=240, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)
ModelCNN_LSTM(
  (conv1): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (conv2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (convs): Sequential(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): ReLU()
    (3): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (4): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (5): LayerNorm((30, 32), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): ReLU()
    (7): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, num_layers=3, batch_first=True)
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=480, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
    (5): LayerNorm((3,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): Linear(in_features=3, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)
ModelLeNet(
  (cnn_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)

    (2): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (3): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (5): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (6): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (7): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (8): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)

ModelCNN_LSTM(
  (conv1): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (conv2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (convs): Sequential(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): ReLU()
    (3): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (4): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (5): LayerNorm((30, 32), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): ReLU()
    (7): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, batch_first=True)
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=480, out_features=256, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=64, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=3, bias=True)
    (5): LayerNorm((3,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): Linear(in_features=3, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

    (2): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (3): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (5): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (6): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (7): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (8): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=240, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

    (4): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

    (6): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(5,), stride=(1,), padding=(2,), groups=30)
    (7): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (8): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )

    (0): Linear(in_features=1920, out_features=2048, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((2048,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

ModelCNN_LSTM(
  (conv1): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (conv2): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
  (convs): Sequential(
    (0): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (1): LayerNorm((30, 64), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): ReLU()
    (3): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (4): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (5): LayerNorm((30, 32), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): ReLU()
    (7): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, batch_first=True)
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=480, out_features=256, bias=True)
    (1): LayerNorm((256,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=64, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=3, bias=True)
    (5): LayerNorm((3,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): Linear(in_features=3, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

    (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=64, bias=True)
    (3): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=3, bias=True)
    (5): LayerNorm((3,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): Linear(in_features=3, out_features=3, bias=True)
  )
  (dropout): Dropout(p=0, inplace=False)
)

    (2): ReLU()
    (3): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
    (4): Conv1d(30, 30, kernel_size=(3,), stride=(1,), padding=(1,), groups=30)
    (5): LayerNorm((30, 32), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
    (6): ReLU()
    (7): MaxPool1d(kernel_size=2, stride=2, padding=0, dilation=1, ceil_mode=False)
  )
  (lstm): LSTM(30, 30, batch_first=True)
  (fc_layers): ModuleList(
